class="withdrawal-modal-body"><p class="withdrawal-modal-subtitle">Als uw gegevens overeenkomen met een bestelling, ontvangt u een e-mail met een link om deze te bekijken en te beheren.</p></div><div class="withdrawal-modal-footer"><button class="withdrawal-btn-submit withdrawal-btn-got-it" type="button">Ik snap het</button></div></div></div></div><script>
(function () {
  var wrapper   = document.getElementById('withdrawal-lookup-modal-wrapper');
  var submitBtn = document.getElementById('withdrawal-submit-btn');
  var emailInput     = document.getElementById('withdrawal-email');
  var orderInput     = document.getElementById('withdrawal-order-number');
  var emailError     = document.getElementById('withdrawal-email-error');
  var orderError     = document.getElementById('withdrawal-order-error');
  var formSection    = document.getElementById('withdrawal-modal-form-section');
  var successSection = document.getElementById('withdrawal-modal-success');

  function openModal() {
    wrapper.classList.add('is-open');
    emailInput.focus();
  }

  function closeModal() {
    wrapper.classList.remove('is-open');
    resetModal();
  }

  function resetModal() {
    emailInput.value = '';
    orderInput.value = '';
    clearError(emailInput, emailError);
    clearError(orderInput, orderError);
    formSection.style.display = '';
    successSection.style.display = 'none';
    submitBtn.disabled = false;
    submitBtn.textContent = 'Bestelling zoeken';
    wrapper.setAttribute('aria-labelledby', 'withdrawal-modal-title-form');
  }

  function showError(input, errorEl, msg) {
    input.classList.add('has-error');
    errorEl.textContent = msg;
    errorEl.style.display = 'block';
  }

  function clearError(input, errorEl) {
    input.classList.remove('has-error');
    errorEl.textContent = '';
    errorEl.style.display = 'none';
  }

  function isValidEmail(val) {
    return /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(val);
  }

  function validate() {
    var valid = true;
    var email = emailInput.value.trim();
    var order = orderInput.value.trim();

    clearError(emailInput, emailError);
    clearError(orderInput, orderError);

    if (!email) {
      showError(emailInput, emailError, 'E-mailadres is vereist');
      valid = false;
    } else if (!isValidEmail(email)) {
      showError(emailInput, emailError, 'Geef een geldig e-mail adres op alstublieft.');
      valid = false;
    }

    if (!order) {
      showError(orderInput, orderError, 'Bestelnummer is verplicht.');
      valid = false;
    }

    return valid;
  }

  function showSuccess() {
    formSection.style.display = 'none';
    successSection.style.display = 'block';
    wrapper.setAttribute('aria-labelledby', 'withdrawal-modal-title-success');
  }

  function submit() {
    if (!validate()) return;

    submitBtn.disabled = true;
    submitBtn.textContent = 'Searching...';

    var formData = new FormData();
    formData.append('withdrawal_lookup[email]', emailInput.value.trim());
    formData.append('withdrawal_lookup[order_number]', orderInput.value.trim());

    fetch("https://www.bierloods22.nl/nl/services/withdrawalLookup/", {
      method: 'POST',
      body: formData,
    })
    .then(showSuccess)
    .catch(showSuccess);
  }

  // Open modal when any link to withdrawal-lookup is clicked
  document.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
    var el = e.target.closest('a');
    if (el && el.href && (el.href.indexOf('withdrawal-lookup') !== -1)) {
      e.preventDefault();
      openModal();
    }
  });

  // Close on backdrop, close button, cancel button, got-it button
  wrapper.querySelector('.withdrawal-modal-background').addEventListener('click', closeModal);
  wrapper.querySelectorAll('.withdrawal-modal-close, .withdrawal-btn-cancel, .withdrawal-btn-got-it').forEach(function (el) {
    el.addEventListener('click', closeModal);
  });

  // ESC key
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
    if (e.key === 'Escape' && wrapper.classList.contains('is-open')) closeModal();
  });

  // Submit
  document.getElementById('withdrawal-lookup-form').addEventListener('submit', function (e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    submit();
  });

  // Live clear errors on input
  emailInput.addEventListener('input', function () { clearError(emailInput, emailError); });
  orderInput.addEventListener('input', function () { clearError(orderInput, orderError); });
}());
</script><!-- [END] 'blocks/body.rain' --><div class="newsletter gray-bg"><h3><i class="fa fa-paper-plane" aria-hidden="true"></i> Meld je aan voor onze nieuwsbrief
        </h3><div class="newsletter-sub">Ontvang de nieuwste aanbiedingen en promoties</div><form action="https://www.bierloods22.nl/nl/account/newsletter/" method="post" id="form-newsletter"><input type="hidden" name="key" value="42b63cda728ba0941f290f1b74b7000d" /><div class="input"><input type="email" name="email" id="emailaddress" value="" placeholder="E-mailadres" /></div><span class="submit button-bg" onclick="$('#form-newsletter').submit();"><i class="fa fa-envelope"></i> Abonneer</span></form></div><footer class=""><div class="container footer"><div class="row"><div class="col-md-3 col-sm-6 company-info rowmargin p-compact"><h3>Speciaalbier winkel Bierloods22</h3><p class="contact-description">Bezoek onze winkel:</p><p class="info"><i class="fas fa-map-marker-alt"></i> Voorstraat 22<br>
